				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Herz und Mund und Tat und Leben, BWV 147 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Herz und Mund und Tat und Leben
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Heart and mouth and deed and life
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="zh-hans">心、口、行止与生活</span>; <span title="zh-hant, zh-hk, zh">心、口、行止與生活</span>; <span title="pt">Herz und Mund und Tat und Leben, BWV 147a</span>; <span title="ca">Cantata núm. 147</span>; <span title="ja">心と口と行いと生活で</span>; <span title="he">Herz und Mund und Tat und Leben, רי"ב 147</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
</th>
<td><span title="fr">Jésus que ma joie demeure</span>; <span title="ca">Cantata núm. 147 de Bach</span>; <span title="ca">El cor, la boca, l'acció i la vida</span>; <span title="ja">心と口と行いと生きざまをもて</span>; <span title="ja">主よ、人の望みの喜びを</span>; <span class="expandline" title="2 more..."><span title="ja">心と口と行いと生活もて</span>; <span title="ja">主よ、人の望みの喜びよ</span></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/186282225">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herz_und_Mund_und_Tat_und_Leben,_BWV_147">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/186282225">186282225</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_of_Congress_Control_Number" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Library of Congress Control Number">LCCN</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://id.loc.gov/authorities/names/n82039521">n82039521</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300008449">300008449</a>; <span class="expandline" title="3 more..."><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb14006639v">14006639v</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/National_Library_of_Australia" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:National Library of Australia">NLA</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://nla.gov.au/anbd.aut-an35610523">35610523</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioteca_Nacional_de_Espa%C3%B1a" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Biblioteca Nacional de España">BNE</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogo.bne.es/uhtbin/authoritybrowse.cgi?action=display&amp;authority_id=XX2526144">XX2526144</a></span>

<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 147&#160;; BC A 174
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 790
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>C major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>10 movements (in 2 parts):
<dl><dt><ul><li>Parte prima
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>1. Chorus: Herz und Mund und Tat und Leben
</dd><dd>2. Recitativo (tenor): Gebenedeiter Mund!
</dd><dd>3. Aria (alto): Schäme dich, o Seele nicht
</dd><dd>4. Recitativo (bass): Verstockung kann Gewaltige verblenden
</dd><dd>5. Aria (soprano): Bereite dir, Jesu, noch itzo die Bahn
</dd><dd>6. Chorale: Wohl mir, daß ich Jesum habe
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>Parte seconda
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>7. Aria (tenor): Hilf, Jesu, hilf, daß ich auch dich bekenne
</dd><dd>8. Recitativo (alto): Der höchsten Allmacht Wunderhand
</dd><dd>9. Aria (bass): Ich will von Jesu Wundern singen
</dd><dd>10. Chorale: Jesus bleibet meine Freude
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1723 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>

<td>1723-07-02 in Leipzig (1st Performance)<br />1730-07-02 ca. in Leipzig (2nd Performance)<br />1735-40 in Leipzig (3rd Performance)
